<p class=MsoTitle><span lang=EN-US>P3 Wrangle Data</span></p>

<p class=MsoSubtitle><span lang=EN-US>Udacity Data analyst Training</span></p>

<p class=ContactInfo><span lang=EN-US>Marcus Pauli | p3 Wrangle Data | 26.02.2017<br
clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;page-break-before:always'>
</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:11.25pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:3.75pt;margin-left:
0cm;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:16.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%;color:#007789;
mso-themecolor:accent1;mso-themeshade:191'>Reviewer notes:<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>As the project did not state out to use an
explicit technology, I did all that with a virtual Ubuntu version. How to
accomplish the whole task with the Anaconda/Notebook looked far too complicated
and would have needed even more time to accomplish.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Thus I did it with below mentioned tools
and the additions within the appendix to accomplish the actual SQL statements
and results to get the results to complete the project.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The SQL statements are written down within
this document.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The actual SQL-DB is uploaded to the GitHUB
as ZIP file.</span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:11.25pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:3.75pt;margin-left:
0cm;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:16.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%;color:#007789;
mso-themecolor:accent1;mso-themeshade:191'>Target 1: Choose Your Map Area<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Choose any area of the world from<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="https://www.openstreetmap.org/#map=5/51.500/-0.100" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>https://www.openstreetmap.org</span></b></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>, and download a XML OSM dataset. The dataset should
be at least 50MB in size (uncompressed). We recommend using one of following
methods of downloading a dataset:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:14.2pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo16;
tab-stops:list 36.0pt;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.5pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Download a preselected metro area from<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="https://mapzen.com/data/metro-extracts/" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Map Zen</span></b></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:14.2pt;mso-list:l16 level1 lfo16;
tab-stops:list 36.0pt;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.5pt;font-family:Symbol;
mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Use the<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="http://overpass-api.de/query_form.html" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Overpass API</span></b></a><span
class=apple-converted-space><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>to download a custom square area. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Explanation
of the syntax can found in the<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="http://wiki.openstreetmap.org/wiki/Overpass_API" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>wiki</span></b></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>. In general you will want to use
the following query:(node(minimum_latitude, minimum_longitude,
maximum_latitude, maximum_longitude);&lt;;);out meta; e.g.
(node(51.249,7.148,51.251,7.152);&lt;;);out meta; the meta option is included
so the elements contain timestamp and user information. You can use the Open
Street Map<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="http://www.openstreetmap.org/export#map=5/42.618/-7.559" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Export Tool</span></b></a><span
class=apple-converted-space><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>to find the coordinates of your bounding box.<span
class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span><em><span style='font-family:"inherit",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial'>Note: You will not be able to use the Export Tool
to actually download the data, the area required for this project is too large.</span></em><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h3 style='margin-top:11.25pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:3.75pt;margin-left:
0cm;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:16.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%;color:#007789;
mso-themecolor:accent1;mso-themeshade:191'>Solution:<o:p></o:p></span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
background:#FDFDFD;word-break:break-all'><span lang=EN-US>The Area of southern
Bavaria in Germany was chosen as data source and the data was </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
background:#FDFDFD;word-break:break-all'><span lang=EN-US>downloaded
accordingly from: </span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";color:#333333;mso-fareast-language:
DE'><a
href="http://download.geofabrik.de/europe/germany/bayern/oberbayern-latest.osm.bz2">http://download.geofabrik.de/europe/germany/bayern/oberbayern-latest.osm.bz2</a><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;
tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
background:#FDFDFD;word-break:break-all'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
color:#333333;mso-fareast-language:DE'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Target 2: Process your Dataset</span></h2>

<p style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:11.25pt;margin-left:
0cm;background:white;vertical-align:baseline'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>It is recommended that you start with the problem sets
in your chosen course and modify them to suit your chosen data set. As you
unravel the data, take note of problems encountered along the way as well as
issues with the dataset. You are going to need these when you write your
project report.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US>SQL</span></h2>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Thoroughly audit and clean your dataset,
converting it from XML to CSV format. Then import the cleaned .csv files into a
SQL database using<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="https://gist.github.com/swwelch/f1144229848b407e0a5d13fcb7fbbd6f"
target="_blank"><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>this schema</span></b></a><span
class=apple-converted-space><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>&nbsp;</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>or a custom schema of your choice.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Solution</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>With postgresql and PostGIS</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Prepare postgres for the data</span></p>

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Answering Questions on the datasource:</span></h2>

<p class=MsoSubtitle align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US>Find
restaurants within southern bavaria:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;line-height:normal;

style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Consolas;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Target 3: Explore your Database</span></h2>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>After
building your local database you’ll explore your data by running queries. Make
sure to document these queries and their results in the submission document
described below. See the<span class=apple-converted-space>&nbsp;</span></span><a
href="https://review.udacity.com/#!/projects/3168208620/rubric" target="_blank"><b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:
Arial;color:#02B3E4;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Project Rubric</span></b></a><span
class=apple-converted-space><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;
font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>for more information about query expectations.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;
mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;color:#4F4F4F;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:
baseline'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.5pt;font-family:"inherit",serif;

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Target 4: Document your Work</span></h2>

<p style='margin:0cm;margin-bottom:.0001pt;background:white;vertical-align:

<h2><span lang=EN-US>Solution:</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This document is my documentation, the data
is been held within this document. The source data was far too big for GitHUB.</span></p>

<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:110%;font-family:"Constantia",serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:Constantia;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span>

--defaults-file=&quot;c:\users\mpauli~1.ccs\appdata\local\temp\tmpetkjmq.cnf&quot;<span

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US>CREATE TABLE
`member_node` (</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>`nodeid` int(11) NOT NULL,</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>`relid` int(11) NOT NULL,</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>`role` varchar(255) NOT NULL,</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>KEY `wayid` (`nodeid`,`relid`)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US>) ENGINE=InnoDB
DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
DE'>CREATE TABLE `nodes` (<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:normal'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
